2026-03-31T21:11:03Z #11 484.3 
2026-03-31T21:11:03Z #11 484.3 
2026-03-31T21:11:03Z #11 484.3 On Linux, Open MPI is built with CUDA awareness but it is disabled by default.
2026-03-31T21:11:03Z #11 484.3 To enable it, please set the environment variable
2026-03-31T21:11:03Z #11 484.3 OMPI_MCA_opal_cuda_support=true
2026-03-31T21:11:03Z #11 484.3 before launching your MPI processes.
2026-03-31T21:11:03Z #11 484.3 Equivalently, you can set the MCA parameter in the command line:
2026-03-31T21:11:03Z #11 484.3 mpiexec --mca opal_cuda_support 1 ...
2026-03-31T21:11:03Z #11 484.3 Note that you might also need to set UCX_MEMTYPE_CACHE=n for CUDA awareness via
2026-03-31T21:11:03Z #11 484.3 UCX. Please consult UCX documentation for further details.
